# Production readiness: the MC compiler (`mcc`)

Status: **qualified subset, not generally production-ready**.
Current assessment: **updated 2026-07-16, based on the current compiler worktree**.
Evidence register: **686 bounded implementation or regression entries, 0 active slices, 3 open architectural workstreams**.

The compiler has locally verified behavior across its supported subset. It is not
ready for an unrestricted production claim because pointer-provenance race
lowering, typed-MIR ownership of semantic facts, and CFG/place-based move analysis
still have open architectural closure boundaries.

The evidence count is an audit register, not a completion percentage. The three
closure matrices below, rather than the evidence count, define the exit criteria
for a general production-ready claim.

## 0. Current Assessment

### Product Positioning

As of 2026-07-11, MC is best described as a **kernel-profile,
freestanding-oriented machine-contract language prototype**, not as a generally
production-ready language competing head-on with Zig, Odin, C, C++, or Rust for
all systems-programming use cases.

The compiler's most important value is not Zig-like syntax. It is the attempt to
make low-level machine contracts explicit and locally checkable:

- arithmetic domains such as checked, wrapping, saturating, serial, and counter
  arithmetic;
- address/resource types such as `PAddr`, `VAddr`, `DmaAddr`, and `MmioPtr`;
- MMIO, DMA/cache ownership, IRQ context, and freestanding trap contracts;
- opt-in `move` resources for linear hardware/resource capabilities;
- explicit machine-effect attributes such as `#[no_lang_trap]`,
  `#[bounded]`, and `#[irq_context]`;
- the rule that optimization mode must not silently change the semantics of an
  already accepted program.

The supported-subset claim should therefore be read as a kernel/freestanding
compiler qualification claim. It is not a claim that MC already has the full
toolchain maturity, package ecosystem, metaprogramming breadth, module system,
separate compilation story, or general memory-safety model expected from a
general-purpose production language.

### Strategic Constraint

The project should stop treating additional surface-language features as the
main path to production readiness. The current readiness risk is architectural:
the language surface is already large enough, while the compiler's semantic
authority is still converging from AST/backend-local inference toward typed
facts and MIR-owned decisions.

The practical rule is:

> Backends may use syntax to choose emission shape, but type, provenance,
> ownership, effect, ABI, representation, and safety decisions must come from
> typed semantic facts or MIR-owned state. When the fact is missing, lowering
> must be conservative or the source must be rejected with a diagnostic.

Longer-term designs such as `shared<T>`, restricted lifetime/region checking,
`unsafe fn`, trait-qualified method namespaces, a true module graph, and
bounded structural reflection are part of the broader production-readiness
track. They are listed in the design-risk readiness table below. The three
workstreams below remain the current compiler-implementation blockers for the
supported subset; the design-risk table defines additional decisions required
before a broad language/product production claim.

### Current Guarantee

Within the tested supported subset, the compiler either emits the documented
lowering or rejects unsupported cases explicitly. Unknown scalar pointer
dereferences use conservative race-tolerant lowering where supported.

This document does not claim complete correctness for arbitrary pointer-return
flow, arbitrary aggregate-return CFG, or general CFG-based move ownership.

### Evidence Model

- A **finished** row means one bounded behavior or regression-evidence slice is
  locally verified and tied to concrete evidence. Evidence-only rows must say so;
  they do not advance an umbrella's closure matrix by themselves.
- An **active** row means one bounded behavior is actively being changed and
  still needs evidence before it can move to finished. It is not counted as
  completed evidence and must not change the supported-subset claim.
- An **open architectural workstream** is larger than one implementation slice. Its
  count should not drop just because another narrow case lands; it drops only
  when the workstream's acceptance boundary is either fully closed or explicitly
  narrowed by project decision.
- Historical sections after the evidence register are audit context. When they
  conflict with this assessment, this assessment is the current source of truth.
- The open-workstream count is not a percentage. The workstreams overlap but
  are not interchangeable; progress is reported by closure-matrix rows, not by
  adding completed evidence entries.

### Evidence Register

| Item | Why it matters | Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| Parser nesting is bounded | Deep input now produces a diagnostic instead of a compiler crash. | `E_NESTING_TOO_DEEP`; direct deep-paren probe rejects cleanly. |
| Parser recovery reports multiple parse errors across scoped bodies | Top-level declarations, block statements, module/impl/trait members, and aggregate fields now resync inside the enclosing syntax body; parse-failed modules still abort before sema, avoiding misleading semantic follow-on errors. | `7d705b12 Improve parser declaration recovery`; `tests/spec/parser_statement_recovery.mc`; `tests/spec/parser_declaration_recovery.mc`; direct `mcc check` emits multiple parse diagnostics without orphan-brace noise. |
| Missing imports and cross-file diagnostics are actionable | Users see the failing import path or imported file/line instead of root-file noise or raw Zig traces. | `E_IMPORT_NOT_FOUND` probe; imported `lib.mc` diagnostic points at `lib.mc`. |
| Expected diagnostic failures no longer print Zig error-return traces | Normal user errors no longer look like compiler ICEs. | Unknown identifier probe prints only the MC diagnostic. |
| Monomorphization has limits and generic body prechecks | Polymorphic recursion and invalid instantiated operators fail loudly instead of hanging or reaching backend emission. | `E_MONOMORPHIZATION_LIMIT`; `38eff033 Validate generic instantiation operators in sema`. |
| Closure typing and closure escape checks are enforced | Closure calls cannot silently use the wrong signature or dangling environment. | `tests/spec/closure_typing.mc`; pushed closure soundness fixes. |
| Linear move checks cover loop conditions and short-circuit RHS | Move-only resources cannot be conditionally consumed in a way that leaks or double-frees. | `tests/spec/move_linear.mc`; `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH` probes. |
| Aggregate `uninit` reads are tracked | Struct/array `var x: T = uninit` reads no longer compile before definite initialization. | `tests/spec/initialization.mc`; `tests/c_emit/bad/use_before_init_aggregate.mc`. |
| Extern/export struct-by-value ABI hazards fail closed | Unsupported C ABI aggregate passing is rejected instead of mislowered by LLVM. | `tests/c_emit/bad/extern_struct_return_by_value.mc`; `tests/c_emit/bad/export_struct_return_by_value.mc`. |
| 128-bit comptime/reflection overflow is guarded | Huge layout/reflection expressions return diagnostics instead of panicking the compiler. | `tests/spec/reflection.mc`; `src/eval_tests.zig` array-size helper tests. |
| `cstr` is implemented and documented | The normative FFI string type now exists across sema, MIR, C, and LLVM lowering. | `1f5c0274 Implement cstr FFI type`; `7278d844 docs: sync cstr FFI status`. |
| Async control-flow spec matches implementation | The spec no longer claims completed E3a/E3b/E3c async forms are reserved. | `b4650dab docs: sync async control-flow spec`; `zig build test`. |
| KASAN/KMSAN store-side sanitizer gaps are closed | Sanitizer modes catch freed/uninitialized heap state on stores as well as loads. | `5b25e328`, `ba8b8de9`. |
| LLVM direct global race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Direct global scalar, struct-field, and array-element accesses now lower to unordered LLVM atomics instead of plain `load`/`store`. | `9ca762fc Lower racing globals to unordered LLVM atomics`; `llvm-as` on `data_race_semantics` IR. |
| LLVM bounded pointer-mediated global race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Direct `(&global).*` and local pointer slots initialized from direct global storage, including simple pointer-local copies, lower scalar deref loads/stores to unordered LLVM atomics; broader escaped/computed provenance remains pending. | `cf8b2fdd Lower global pointer derefs to LLVM atomics`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `llvm-as` on `data_race_semantics` IR. |
| LLVM raw-many offset pointer derefs are bounded and conservative | Raw-many pointer locals initialized from already-proven global-backed storage preserve provenance through constant `.offset(0)` and lower the final scalar deref as unordered atomic. Nonzero, dynamic, and unknown call-produced offsets do not claim global provenance, but their scalar derefs now lower conservatively to unordered atomics instead of plain loads. | `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `possibly_racing_raw_many_offset_zero_pointer_load` / `raw_many_offset_one_pointer_lowers_atomic` / `raw_many_offset_dynamic_pointer_lowers_atomic` / `raw_many_offset_unknown_pointer_lowers_atomic`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` raw-many offset assertions; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `pointer_fact_raw_many_nonzero_lowers_race_tolerant` / `pointer_fact_raw_many_dynamic_lowers_race_tolerant` / `pointer_fact_raw_many_unknown_lowers_race_tolerant`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM returned global-pointer race lowering is no longer UB-bearing | Internal helpers proven to return visible global-backed pointer expressions now preserve that provenance at call sites, so scalar derefs of the returned pointer lower to unordered atomics. | `0fb49f96 Lower returned global pointers atomically in LLVM`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `returned_global_pointer`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM scalar pointer-return fallback is retired | LLVM no longer scans function bodies into `global_pointer_return_fns` or treats returned-call expressions as backend-local global proofs. Supported direct, forwarded, noalias-wrapped, branched, local pointer-alias, and local-function-alias return flows are represented by caller MIR facts; missing or unsupported return facts remain unknown and final scalar dereferences use the atomic default. Aggregate-return summaries remain separate. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of `global_pointer_return_fns` and `collectGlobalPointerProvenanceSummaries`; `src/mir.zig` `collectDirectGlobalPointerReturnSummaries`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM consumes MIR facts for direct internal global pointer returns`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM global pointer-local fallback is retired | C pointer-like local initialization and reassignment are MIR-only. LLVM removes its final `updatePointerGlobalProvenance` ladder: covered direct forms without a MIR fact remain unknown and lower atomically. LLVM retains only a registered local-storage proof for non-MIR aggregate-alias shapes, preserving plain access to storage already proven local without recreating a global proof. Aggregate aliases, field facts, arrays, slices, and aggregate-return summaries remain separate bounded mechanisms. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updatePointerProvenanceFromMirOrLocalProof` / `updatePointerProvenanceAssignmentFromMirOrLocalProof`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` MIR-only matching helpers; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` and `src/lower_c_tests.zig` missing-pointer-provenance suites; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Direct local aggregate-pointer aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits normal destination facts for direct field and constant-index pointer-array reads through a local alias initialized from `&local_aggregate`. Alias writes retain an alias-scoped field fact while invalidating the original aggregate path, so direct and alias reads remain conservative where the existing semantics require it. C and LLVM consume the destination facts; deleting one makes the final scalar access race-tolerant rather than rebuilding an alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` local aggregate alias map and alias-scoped field facts; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records direct local aggregate pointer alias provenance facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` local aggregate alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| Direct local fixed-pointer-array aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits a normal destination fact for a constant-index read through a local pointer initialized directly from `&ptrs`, such as `pa.*[0]`. A write through the alias invalidates the backing array facts; dynamic alias indexes remain in the separate all-elements fallback boundary. C and LLVM consume the destination fact, and deleting it makes the final scalar access race-tolerant rather than rebuilding LLVM's local pointer-array alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` local pointer-array alias map and invalidation; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records direct local pointer-array alias provenance facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` local pointer-array alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| Dynamic all-elements local fixed-pointer-array aliases are MIR-owned | MIR now emits a destination fact for `pa.*[i]` when every backing pointer-array element has the same live `local_storage` or `global_storage` provenance. Mixed, invalidated, and reassigned aliases remain unknown. C and LLVM consume the destination fact; deleting it makes the scalar dereference race-tolerant rather than using LLVM's all-elements alias proof. | `src/mir.zig` `dynamicLocalPointerArrayAliasElementProvenance` / `allLivePointerArrayElementProvenance`; `src/mir_tests.zig` dynamic all-local/all-global/mixed alias cases; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` dynamic local pointer-array alias missing-destination suites; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM scalar pointer parameters fail closed without MIR facts | Scalar pointer parameter call-site summaries, including direct and function-pointer-alias call paths, no longer seed LLVM-local global/local provenance. In the absence of a typed MIR parameter fact, scalar parameter derefs use the established unordered-atomic default, matching the aggregate parameter policy. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of scalar parameter summary collection/seeding; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `consume_global_param` / `consume_local_only_param` / `consume_indirect_local_param`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM direct scalar parameter summaries are retired | A direct internal call that passes `&global` or `&local` no longer grants the callee's scalar pointer parameter a backend-local provenance proof. Both paths lower atomically unless a future typed MIR parameter fact supplies a positive local proof. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of `global_pointer_params` and scalar parameter seeding; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `consume_global_param` / `consume_local_only_param`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM scalar function-pointer parameter inference is retired | Local function-pointer aliases no longer form backend-local scalar parameter provenance proofs. Direct, copied, reassigned, escaped, mixed, and uncalled scalar parameter shapes all remain safe through atomic lowering until a typed MIR parameter-summary family exists. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removal of scalar parameter call-site collector; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` scalar parameter fixtures; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "ordinary global scalar accesses"`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM function-pointer alias parameter inference is retired | LLVM no longer follows local function-pointer aliases to infer pointer parameter provenance. Without a typed MIR parameter fact, scalar and aggregate pointer parameter dereferences use the conservative atomic path, so they do not depend on LLVM-local call-site inference. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` removed parameter alias collectors; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM aggregate-contained pointer field race lowering is no longer UB-bearing for bounded local fields | Direct local aggregate pointer fields initialized or assigned from visible global storage now seed local pointer copies as global-backed during LLVM emission; stack-backed, reassigned stack-backed, whole-aggregate copy, and exported-return ambiguity cases remain plain. | `49f02b3f Track aggregate pointer field provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_global_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_reassigned_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_whole_copy_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_exported_return_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM aggregate whole-copy pointer field provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct same-struct local-to-local aggregate assignment/init copies now propagate already-proven pointer-field facts, so copied global-backed fields continue to lower derefs as unordered atomics while stack-backed and computed aggregate sources remain plain. | `352be47f Propagate aggregate copy pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_whole_copy_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_init_copy_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_whole_copy_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_computed_copy_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM nested aggregate pointer field provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local named member paths such as `outer.inner.ptr` now carry proven global-backed pointer-field facts through struct-literal init and direct nested field assignment; stack-backed and reassigned-stack nested paths remain plain. | `fd48f50a Track nested aggregate pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `nested_aggregate_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_assigned_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `nested_aggregate_reassigned_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local pointer-array provenance is bounded and conservative | Direct local fixed arrays of pointer-like elements now carry proven global-backed facts for constant-index literal elements and constant-index assignments; stack-backed elements and dynamic-index reads/writes remain plain. | `9f24297e Track LLVM local array pointer provenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_global_pointer_element_load` / `array_assigned_global_pointer_element_load` / `array_stack_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `array_dynamic_index_pointer_element_stays_plain` / `array_dynamic_assignment_clears_pointer_element_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |
| LLVM local aggregate-pointer aliases are bounded and conservative | Local pointer variables declared directly from `&local_aggregate` now resolve member-path pointer facts through the original aggregate, including nested paths; stack-backed fields, returned/external aggregate pointers, and reassigned unknown aliases remain plain. Aggregate pointer parameters without MIR facts are not local aliases and lower final scalar dereferences atomically. | `f4f13294 Track local aggregate pointer aliases in LLVM`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `aggregate_pointer_alias_global_pointer_field_load` / `nested_aggregate_pointer_alias_global_pointer_field_load` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_stack_pointer_field_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_returned_unknown_stays_plain` / `aggregate_pointer_param_field_lowers_atomic` / `aggregate_pointer_alias_reassigned_unknown_lowers_atomic`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`. |

| LLVM all-local direct pointer-array dynamic reads preserve local provenance | LLVM now keeps `local_storage` as a first-class fixed local pointer-array element fact instead of collapsing non-global elements to unknown. Dynamic reads from direct local fixed pointer arrays, and from direct local pointer-to-array aliases backed by all-local elements, seed the destination pointer local as proven local so the final scalar deref stays plain; partial/global, reassigned, slice-backed, and aggregate-backed dynamic reads remain conservative. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `local_array_global_pointer_elements` stores `mir.PointerProvenance`, `localArrayAllElementsHaveLocalPointerProvenance`, `directLocalArrayBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`, `localPointerArrayAliasBaseHasAllLocalPointerProvenance`; `tests/spec/data_race_semantics.mc` `array_dynamic_index_all_local_pointer_elements_stays_plain` / `pointer_to_array_stack_pointer_elements_stays_plain`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM all-local aggregate pointer-array dynamic reads preserve local provenance | LLVM aggregate pointer-field facts now preserve `local_storage` as well as `global_storage`. | Typed semantic facts inventory rejects global provenance fallback | The semantic-facts inventory now enforces zero LLVM `updatePointerGlobalProvenance` definitions and calls. | Target-dependent expression, explicit-cast, and view const-narrowing types are MIR-owned | MIR records complete `ast.TypeExpr`, compressed result type, kind, and source point for contextual constructors, mapped-try error expressions, null/optional/dyn coercions, typed literals/aggregates, both sides of every explicit cast, and both sides of implicit `*mut T` to `*const T` / `[]mut T` to `[]const T` narrowing. A `? else MAPPED` expression is built with the enclosing `Result<T,E>` error type, closing the mapped enum-literal gap exposed after backend enum inference was retired. Cast source production covers typed values, contextual literals/aggregates, arithmetic, bitcast/unchecked/conversion/semantic-escape calls, and address-of values; generated pointer type nodes are owned and freed by the MIR function. Implicit narrowing facts cover return, local-initializer, and call-argument contexts; pass-through views and raw-many pointers produce no narrowing facts. C runtime cast emission, C slice const reinterpretation, C cast-result queries, LLVM runtime casts, LLVM global cast initializers, LLVM cast-result typing, and LLVM no-op view coercion consume the paired facts instead of `node.ty`, `exprType(value)`, or C operand inference as semantic authority. Missing cast or narrowing facts reject prebuilt MIR in both backends. Existing optional/dyn pass-through and nested aggregate multiplicity rules remain unchanged. | `src/mir_model.zig` explicit-cast and `view_const_narrow_*` `TargetTypeKind` cases plus generated type-node ownership; `src/mir.zig` mapped-try `buildExprWithTargetType`, `explicitCastSourceTypeExpr` / `explicitCastCallSourceTypeExpr`, and `isViewConstNarrowCast` target-fact producer; C `emitCastExpr` / `emitSliceConstNarrowCoercion`; LLVM `emitCast` / `emitGlobalInitializer` / `coerceExprValue` / `exprType`; MIR mapped-try and narrowing positive/pass-through/raw-many tests; C/LLVM missing-cast and missing-narrowing-fact tests; `tryelse-test` backend parity; contextual enum-cast and full-suite leak evidence; semantic-facts inventory fallback guards; `zig build test`; `zig build c-test llvm-test`; `zig build diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| `try` operand types are MIR-owned | Every accepted `?` expression records one complete `try_operand` fact for its Result or nullable operand. C's direct, nested, sequenced, and hoisted `try` paths select Result versus nullable lowering and materialize the operand from that fact. LLVM requires the same fact before unwrapping and uses it for `try` expression result typing. Missing facts fail generic MIR admission; stale facts fail backend emission. This closes only `try` operand classification, not mapped-error typing, broader expression typing, or the typed-HIR/MIR workstream. | `src/mir_model.zig` `try_operand`; `src/mir.zig` `buildExpr` try producer; `src/lower_c_try.zig` `tryOperandType` / `resultTryOperandType` / `nullableTryOperandCType`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` try scans; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirTryOperandType`; MIR/C/LLVM missing/stale fact tests; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig build test c-test llvm-test`; `git diff --check`. |
| `for` iterable and element types are MIR-owned | Every accepted `for` loop records complete `for_iterable` and `for_element` facts. C uses them to materialize call-bearing iterables and type the loop binding; LLVM uses them for iterable storage, length, element load, and binding storage. Both backends validate that the two facts agree structurally before emission. Missing facts fail generic MIR admission; stale facts fail backend emission. This closes only `for` iterable/element typing, not broader expression typing or the typed-HIR/MIR workstream. | `src/mir_model.zig` `for_iterable` / `for_element`; `src/mir.zig` `buildLoop`; C `requireMirForLoopTypes` / `lower_c_flow`; LLVM `requireMirForLoopTypes`; MIR/C/LLVM array/slice/call and missing/stale fact tests; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig build test c-test llvm-test`; `git diff --check`. |
| Direct-call inferred-local types are MIR-owned | A one-name unannotated local initialized by an ordinary direct function or extern call now carries an owned `inferred_local` fact in addition to the call's existing result fact. C and LLVM use that local fact to allocate/type the destination binding; they consult the declared call result only to reject stale prebuilt MIR. C's array, slice, tagged-union, Result, and nullable direct-call initializer paths all consume the same destination fact when present instead of bypassing it through their specialized type classifiers. Builtins, non-dynamic member calls, and other computed initializers remain in the registered expression-inference boundary. | `src/mir.zig` `inferredLocalCallType`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` direct-call inferred initializer paths / `emitCallInferredLocalInit`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirInferredLocalType`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR owns inferred local direct call types`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` scalar and Result direct-call inferred-local missing/stale tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| Indirect-call inferred-local types are MIR-owned | A one-name unannotated local initialized by a function-pointer or closure call now carries an owned `inferred_local` fact derived from the call's complete `indirect_call_callee` signature fact. C and LLVM use the destination fact for allocation, then require it to agree with that callee-signature result. Missing destination facts fail generic MIR admission; a destination fact retargeted away from the pointer/closure result fails both backends. Non-dynamic member calls, builtins, and other computed initializers remain outside this bounded migration. | `src/mir.zig` `inferredLocalCallType` / `indirectCallTarget`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitCallInferredLocalInit`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `requireMirInferredLocalType` / `inferredLocalCallReturnType`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR owns inferred local indirect call types`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` indirect-call inferred-local complete/missing/stale tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| Dynamic-dispatch result and fixed-argument types are MIR-owned | Every `*dyn Trait` method call records one `dyn_dispatch_argument` fact for each fixed user argument, keyed by trait name plus an encoded vtable slot/argument index. Non-`void` calls also record `dyn_dispatch_result`; a one-name unannotated local mirrors that result in an owned `inferred_local` fact. This prevents same-named free functions from supplying dynamic-call types. C validates every emitted vtable argument against its MIR fact and trait ABI; LLVM uses those facts to type every emitted argument. Both retain the trait declaration only for ABI/stale-fact validation. Missing facts fail generic MIR admission, while retargeted complete types fail backend emission. Non-dynamic member calls, builtins, variadic dynamic dispatch, and broader computed initializers remain outside this bounded migration. | `src/mir_model.zig` `dyn_dispatch_result` / `dyn_dispatch_argument`; `src/mir.zig` `dynDispatchCallTarget` / `inferredLocalCallType`; `src/lower_c_dispatch.zig` `emitDynDispatch`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` dynamic argument validator; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `emitDynDispatch` / `callReturnType`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR owns inferred local dyn dispatch call types`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` dynamic-dispatch complete/missing/stale tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |

C's direct-read emitter allocates the binding from that destination fact and compares its emitted C type with the established MMIO value type only to reject stale prebuilt MIR; LLVM uses the same destination fact at local admission. MMIO writes remain void and do not create inferred-local result facts. | `src/mir.zig` `inferredLocalCallType` / `mmioCallTarget`; `src/lower_c_mmio.zig` `emitDirectReadInferredLocalInit`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR owns MMIO read write identities and complete types`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` MMIO inferred-local missing/stale tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| Semantic inference family register is gated | Backend semantic inference families that affect type, ABI, representation, bounds, integer/defaulting, call target, ownership, effect, and race/provenance lowering now have a named register with owner/source anchors, current consumers, migration status, and fail-closed policy. The inventory script fails if a registered family row or code anchor drifts. This completes the actionable inventory slice only; it does not migrate the registered families. | `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` `Semantic inference family register`; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py` `SEMANTIC_INFERENCE_FAMILIES`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| Backend AST-inference budget is gated | The typed-facts inventory now has a shrinking exact budget for registered backend AST-inference families. New backend semantic inference families must reuse an existing registered family or deliberately update the budget, and future migration slices must reduce the count when a family stops being backend authority. This completes the budget action slice only; it does not migrate the budgeted families. | `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` `Backend AST-inference budget`; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py` `BACKEND_AST_INFERENCE_BUDGET`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM expression type inference is registered | LLVM's local `exprType` / `derefPointeeType` family, including qualified tagged-union constructor result typing, is now explicitly named in the semantic inference register and counted in the backend AST-inference budget instead of remaining an untracked backend-local type authority. This is a tracking and gating slice, not a typed-fact migration: the family still needs later migration or accepted-fallback closure. | `docs/typed-semantic-facts.md` `llvm-expression-type-inference`; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py` `SEMANTIC_INFERENCE_FAMILIES` and `BACKEND_AST_INFERENCE_BUDGET`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `exprType` and `derefPointeeType`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `git diff --check`. |

| Self-typed expression inference is inventory-gated | The semantic-facts inventory removes qualified-union and enum-path AST type queries from both backend inference families, exact-counts the MIR producer and C/LLVM fact consumers, and keeps retired backend-local classifiers at zero. | Semantic-facts exact-count inventory rejects duplicate file keys | The semantic-facts inventory no longer lets a repeated `EXACT_COUNTS` file key silently replace an earlier exact-count block. | Semantic-facts duplicate-key self-check covers annotated inventory maps | The duplicate-key self-check now inspects the annotated `EXACT_COUNTS: ... = {}` assignment form actually used by the script, so a repeated top-level file key is detected before Python can collapse it. | Raw builtin identities and value-result types are MIR-owned | `raw.load<T>(addr)`, `raw.ptr<T>(addr)`, and `raw.store<T>(addr, value)` have exact MIR call identities, and the two value-producing forms obtain their result types from MIR target facts. | Varargs cursor, payload, and result types are completely MIR-owned | Sema now validates the exact `va.start`/`va.arg`/`va.end` shapes, rejects `va.start` outside a variadic function, and requires each cursor to be `&va_list` or `*mut va_list`. | Ordinary direct-call result and fixed argument types are MIR-owned | Identifier-form calls that resolve to a declared ordinary function or extern now record a complete `direct_call_result` fact and one `direct_call_argument` fact for each fixed parameter. Member calls are deliberately excluded so a same-named free-function summary cannot supply their signature. Each fact is keyed by callee owner plus optional fixed-argument index as well as source point, so generated async calls that share source coordinates cannot alias facts from different callees. Variadic tail arguments deliberately receive no invented target type. C consumes these facts in ordinary expression emission, return-type classifiers, left-to-right sequenced calls, and extern nonnull paths; the nonnull temporary uses `direct_call_result`, while its inferred destination separately requires the owned `inferred_local` type and rejects disagreement. The C array/slice inferred-local specializers likewise require `inferred_local` instead of falling back to their direct-call return classifier. LLVM consumes them in value, void/never, return-type, and fixed-argument emission; its `expectedTyForCallArg` helper and direct `fn_sigs` return fallback are retired. Both backends retain declaration lookup only to confirm ABI identity, arity/variadic mechanics, and stale-fact equality. Missing facts fail generic MIR admission and stale complete types fail backend admission. Dynamic dispatch, member-call identity, and globally stable declaration identity remain separate open boundaries. | `src/mir_model.zig` direct-call target kinds and owner/index identity; `src/mir.zig` direct declaration producer and identity-aware validator/dump; `src/lower_c_infer.zig`; `src/lower_c_call.zig`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig`; `src/lower_llvm.zig`; MIR fixed/variadic ownership and same-named member exclusion test; async generated-source collision regression; C/LLVM positive, missing-result, missing-argument, and stale-fact tests; semantic-facts inventory retired LLVM fallback guards; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |

C and LLVM use these facts for local and global initialization and retain AST only to extract the confirmed operand. | Noalias value lowering dispatch is MIR-owned | C and LLVM now enter `compiler.assume_noalias_unchecked` value lowering solely from the exact `assume_noalias` MIR identity and its complete source/result facts. | Enum raw identities and representation types are MIR-owned | Every recognized `<enum-value>.raw()` call now carries an exact `enum_raw` call identity plus complete `enum_raw_source` and `enum_raw_result` type facts. The producer covers accepted closed/open enums, the default `isize` representation, and `Enum.variant.raw()` paths. C and LLVM consume those facts for dispatch, receiver typing, and result typing; C's duplicate open/general enum return classifiers and LLVM's receiver `exprType` plus enum-table repr reconstruction are retired. Removing either identity or type facts rejects prebuilt MIR in both backends. Enum type-alias receivers remain outside the accepted source subset because sema currently diagnoses them as unknown member access. | `src/mir_model.zig` enum raw call/target kinds; `src/mir.zig` `enumRawCallTarget` / `enumRawSourceTypeExpr`; `src/lower_c_builtin_emit.zig`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `enumRawCallInfo`; MIR and C/LLVM closed/open/default/variant-path positive coverage; C/LLVM missing identity/type tests; `tests/c_emit/enum_raw_closed_g25_g27.mc`; semantic-facts exact fallback guards; focused tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| Arithmetic-domain call identities and complete types are MIR-owned | `wrap<T>.residue()` and all seven `serial<T>` / `counter<T>` operations now carry exact MIR call identities plus complete domain, payload, and result type facts; the two bounded-time operations also carry their complete `Duration<T>` interval type. MIR owns generated `Result<Order, AmbiguousSerialOrder>` and `Result<Duration<T>, AmbiguousCounterInterval>` types through explicit lifetime-managed generic argument slices. C and LLVM use these facts for dispatch, operand/result typing, inferred locals, and result construction instead of resolving domain aliases or rebuilding `wrap`, `Duration`, and `Result` types. Missing identities/types and a stale operation identity reject prebuilt MIR in both backends. | `src/mir_model.zig` domain call/target kinds and generated type ownership; `src/mir.zig` `domainCallFactInfo` / `domainCallTarget`; `src/lower_c_arith.zig`; `src/lower_c_domain.zig`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` domain call consumers; MIR all-operation fact assertions; C/LLVM clean, missing, stale, and inferred-local tests; semantic-facts exact fallback guards; focused tests; full gates. |
| `const_get` array, result, and compile-time index semantics are MIR-owned | Every accepted `array.const_get<N>()` records the exact call identity, complete base-array and result-element types, and a dedicated `ConstGetFact.index`; the typed index instruction redundantly carries the same value so backend admission detects missing or stale facts. C and LLVM retain only the confirmed base operand syntax and consume MIR for the emitted index and result typing. LLVM no longer derives the base through `exprType`, resolves the array locally, or recomputes its length/element type; C no longer reads the AST type argument as semantic authority. Alias-array and inferred-local paths are covered. | `src/mir_model.zig` `Instruction.const_index` / `ConstGetFact` / target kinds; `src/mir.zig` `constGetCallTarget`, dump rows, and bidirectional validator; C/LLVM backend admission gates and const-get consumers; MIR dump/type/index assertions; coupled instruction/fact deletion rejection; C/LLVM clean, missing-type, missing-index, and stale-index tests; semantic-facts exact retired-fallback guards; focused and full gates. |
| DMA call identities and complete types are MIR-owned | The complete accepted DMA call family, `cache.clean`, `cache.invalidate`, `DmaBuf.dma_addr`, and `DmaBuf.as_slice`, now records exact MIR call identities plus complete buffer, payload, and result types. The producer resolves aliases and owns the `[]mut T` result of `as_slice`; C and LLVM consume those facts for admission, operand typing, result typing, and emission. LLVM no longer reconstructs `DmaBuf` through `exprType`/`dmaBufInfo`, and C no longer requires an identifier local with a backend `source_ty` to recognize the value operations. C cache operations now also evaluate their buffer operand once before the barrier, matching LLVM instead of dropping operand effects. Missing call/type facts and stale operation identities reject prebuilt MIR in both backends. | `src/mir_model.zig` DMA call/target kinds; `src/mir.zig` `dmaCallFactInfo` / `dmaCallTarget`; `src/lower_c_memory.zig`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` DMA consumers; MIR all-operation identity/type assertions; C operand-evaluation assertion; C/LLVM alias-buffer and inferred-slice positive coverage plus missing/stale fact gates; semantic-facts exact fallback guards; focused tests; `zig build test c-test llvm-test diff-backend`; `git diff --check`. |
| MMIO register call semantics are MIR-owned | Every accepted `MmioPtr<extern mmio struct>` register `read`/`write` call now records an exact operation identity plus complete MMIO struct, register storage, register value, and result types. This preserves the `RegBits<Storage, Value, Access>` storage/value distinction in one semantic source. C and LLVM consume those facts for admission, value/result typing, and emission; they retain only confirmed operand/field syntax and target layout-offset mechanics. Missing identities/types and stale operation identities reject prebuilt MIR, while C's register metadata lookup and LLVM's receiver/field type reconstruction are inventory-forbidden. | `src/mir_model.zig` MMIO call/target kinds; `src/mir.zig` `mmioCallTarget`; `src/lower_c_mmio.zig`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `mmioAccessInfo`; MIR `Reg`/`RegBits` fact assertions; C/LLVM positive plus missing/stale fact gates; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; focused tests; full gates; `git diff --check`. |

| Call-target validation supports generated same-source multiplicity | Async lowering can create more than one semantically distinct constructor with the generated `(0,0)` source point. Call-target admission now compares the number of matching metadata instructions and owned facts, matching the target-type validator: two matching `result_err` rows are valid, while a fact duplicated without its instruction still fails. Different call kinds at one source point remain ambiguous and fail closed. Removing the destination `PointerProvenanceFact` for `p` suppresses the consumed-fact comment and keeps the scalar deref on the conservative race-tolerant path instead of recreating backend-local global provenance. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `appendCheckedCTestWithoutPointerProvenanceFactsForSubject`, `clearPointerProvenanceFactsForFunctionSubject`, and `lower-c aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact"`; `git diff --check`. |
| Typed semantic facts cover aggregate pointer updates from live direct pointer expressions | MIR now records aggregate pointer-field and aggregate pointer-array element provenance when direct aggregate assignments use already-live direct pointer expressions, including pointer-local copies, instead of only visible `&global` / `&local` addresses. C and LLVM consume those field-path facts for direct aggregate derefs, and tests with the aggregate field fact removed keep the deref on the conservative race-tolerant path without a consumed field-provenance comment. | `src/mir.zig` `directPointerProvenance` use in aggregate pointer-field producers; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records aggregate pointer assignments from pointer-local copy facts`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `c_aggregate_field_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `c_aggregate_array_element_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `aggregate_field_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `aggregate_array_element_pointer_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact`; focused C/LLVM aggregate missing-field tests; `git diff --check`. |

| C call/member/index pointer derefs lower race-tolerantly | The C backend no longer falls back to plain `*p` merely because the pointer expression is not a local identifier. `derefPointeeType` now recovers pointee types for call-produced pointers, casts, pointer fields, and pointer array elements, so scalar loads/stores route through `mc_race_load_*` / `mc_race_store_*` unless proven local. | LLVM aggregate-return AST collector is retired | LLVM no longer pre-scans aggregate-return function bodies to rebuild returned pointer-field provenance. `aggregate_return_pointer_fields` is now populated only from MIR `AggregateReturnPointerFact` rows, so unsupported or missing MIR summaries keep returned fields conservative instead of falling back to LLVM-local AST inference. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `collectMirAggregateReturnPointerFieldFacts`; `tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py` rejects the retired collector names; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `python3 tools/toolchain/semantic-facts-inventory.py`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Consistent internal global pointer branch returns are MIR-owned | MIR now joins direct `return &global` exits across an internal helper's terminating `if`/switch arms, including helpers with ordinary value parameters. It emits a caller `PointerProvenanceFact` only when every modeled exit agrees on the same global; mixed return storage or possible fallthrough remains unknown and therefore lowers race-tolerantly. C and LLVM consume the caller fact at the call-result local, while removing it still preserves the conservative path. Exported, callback, loop, and arbitrary return-flow summaries remain pending. | `src/mir.zig` `collectDirectGlobalPointerReturnSummaries`, `directGlobalReturnFlowForBlock`, and `directPointerProvenance`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR joins consistent internal global pointer returns across branches`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` direct-return fact tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| Internal local pointer-return aliases are MIR-owned | Internal helpers that assign a returned pointer through a straight-line local, such as `let gp = &global; return gp;` or reassignment from an already summarized internal pointer-return helper, now participate in `collectDirectGlobalPointerReturnSummaries`. Unsupported assignments and fallthrough control-flow mutation clear the local alias map, so mixed local returns remain unknown. C and LLVM consume the caller `PointerProvenanceFact`, and deleting it keeps scalar dereferences race-tolerant. Callback/exported/nontrivial returned pointers remain outside this slice. | `src/mir.zig` `directGlobalReturnFlowForBlock`, `directGlobalReturnFlowForStmt`, and `directGlobalAddressStorageExprWithLocals`; `src/mir_tests.zig` `MIR records direct internal global pointer return provenance in callers`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `direct internal global pointer returns`; focused MIR/C/LLVM pointer-return tests; `git diff --check`. |
| MIR tracks straight-line local function aliases for proven pointer returns | A local function-pointer alias initialized directly from an internal helper with an existing global-pointer return summary can now seed the call-result `PointerProvenanceFact`. The alias target is dropped on reassignment, indirect store, address escape, and branch/switch/loop control-flow boundaries, so callbacks, escaped aliases, and joined aliases remain unknown and lower race-tolerantly. C and LLVM consume the resulting ordinary caller fact through their existing missing-fact-gated paths. | `src/mir.zig` `local_function_aliases`, `directPointerReturnAliasTarget`, and alias invalidation; `src/mir_tests.zig` local function-alias return provenance; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` / `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` direct-return fact tests; `zig build test`; `git diff --check`. |
| Bounds checks require typed MIR facts | Non-elided array-index and slice bounds checks now record owned `BoundsFact` entries in MIR. | C unchecked arithmetic consumes MIR no-overflow range facts | C lowering has no generic unchecked-arithmetic fallback authorized by AST syntax. | C no-overflow range facts fail closed on target mismatch | C now has an explicit prebuilt-MIR negative test matching the LLVM retargeted-fact regression: changing an otherwise matching `RangeFact.target` suppresses unchecked arithmetic lowering and returns `UnsupportedCEmission`. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `retargetRangeFactsForFunction`, `appendCheckedCTestWithRetargetedRangeFacts`, and `lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact"`. |
| C no-overflow range fact target coverage matches MIR producers | C regression coverage now exercises the MIR range-fact target labels emitted for return values, inferred locals, assignments, call arguments, binary operands, array literal elements, and struct literal fields, and retargets a struct-field fact to prove non-`value` targets fail closed too. This aligns the C typed-fact gate with the existing LLVM target-identity evidence. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact`; expected `MC_MIR_RANGE` comments for `target=value`, `target=inferred`, `target=sum`, `target=call_arg`, `target=binary_operand`, `target=aggregate_element`, and `target=next`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c unchecked arithmetic requires MIR no-overflow range fact"`. |
| C direct raw-many offset derefs lower race-tolerantly | The C backend now covers the sequenced raw-many `.offset(...).*` access class for scalar pointees. Direct local-base offsets can lower inline through `mc_race_load_*`, and call-produced bases are sequenced into pointer temps before a race-tolerant load temp, avoiding the previous plain `*mc_tmp` load for that access class. This is a bounded slice of broader pointer-provenance race lowering, not full closure. | `src/lower_c_access.zig` `emitRawManyOffsetDerefValueTemp`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceLoadTempFromPointerTemp`; `src/lower_c_infer.zig` `derefPointeeType`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `direct_raw_many_offset_lowers_race_tolerant` / `direct_call_raw_many_offset_lowers_race_tolerant`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly | Ordinary scalar field loads/stores through pointer bases, including call-produced aggregate pointers, no longer emit plain `p->field` / `p->field = value` when locality is not proven. Scalar fields route through `mc_race_load_*` / `mc_race_store_*`, pointer-shaped fields use relaxed C atomics, and direct aggregate fields are handled by the recursive aggregate slice below. This is a bounded aggregate access-class slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberLoadExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberStoreStmt`, `exprHasPointerType`, and `memberFieldType`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c pointer member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C nested pointer-member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly | Nested scalar fields reached through pointer bases, such as `p.inner.value` and `external_outer().inner.value`, now build the full field address and use race helpers or relaxed atomics instead of plain C nested field loads/stores. Aggregate-width pointer-member value copies still fail closed. This is a bounded nested aggregate access-class slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `collectPointerMemberPath`, `emitPointerMemberPathAddressExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberLoadExpr`, and `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberStoreStmt`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c nested pointer member scalar access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C pointer-member aggregate value copies lower recursively | Direct and nested aggregate field value copies through ambiguous pointer bases no longer fall through to plain `p->field` aggregate reads/writes and no longer fail closed when every leaf has sound scalar/pointer race-tolerant lowering. C now sequences the pointer root, reconstructs aggregate loads from leaf `mc_race_load_*` / relaxed atomic pointer loads, and splits aggregate stores into leaf stores. Proven-local pointer bases still use the existing plain path; unsupported union-like leaves still fail closed. This is a bounded pointer-member aggregate slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberAggregateExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberAggregateExpr`, aggregate branches in `emitRaceTolerantPointerMemberStoreStmt` / `emitRaceTolerantNestedPointerMemberStoreStmt`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateLoadFromPtr`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateStoreFromPtr`, and `derefPointerHasProvenLocalStorage`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c pointer member aggregate value copies lower field-wise race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer member aggregate"`; `git diff --check`. |
| C proven-local pointer-member aggregate copies stay plain | C now has explicit local-storage evidence for nested pointer-member aggregate stores and loads. When a pointer to an aggregate is proven local, `p.middle.inner = replacement` and `let inner = p.middle.inner` lower as ordinary C aggregate assignment/copy with the MIR local-storage comment and no `mc_race_*` helpers. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `local_pointer_member_aggregate_copy_stays_plain` in `lower-c pointer member aggregate value copies lower field-wise race-tolerantly`; `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `derefPointerHasProvenLocalStorage`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer member aggregate"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM proven-local nested pointer-member aggregate copies stay plain | LLVM now has explicit nested local-storage evidence for pointer-member aggregate stores and loads. | C aggregate pointer deref value copies lower recursively | Aggregate pointee value copies through unproven pointer derefs no longer fall through to plain `*p` aggregate reads or `*p = value` aggregate writes, and no longer fail closed for struct/fixed-array aggregates whose leaves have sound race-tolerant lowering. C now emits a statement-expression pointer temp, reconstructs aggregate loads from `mc_race_load_*` / relaxed atomic pointer leaves, and splits aggregate stores into leaf stores. Proven-local pointer derefs still use the existing plain path; union-like and unsupported leaves still fail closed. This is a bounded aggregate deref slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefExpr`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateLoadFromPtr`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateStoreFromPtr`, `raceAggregateKind`, and aggregate branch in `emitRaceTolerantDerefStoreStmt`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c aggregate pointer deref value copies lower field-wise race-tolerantly` / `lower-c nested aggregate pointer deref value copies lower recursively` / `lower-c fixed-array aggregate pointer deref value copies lower recursively`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| C slice scalar index access lowers race-tolerantly | Scalar element loads and stores through slice indexing no longer emit plain `slice.ptr[checked_index]` access when storage is ambiguous. | MIR representation facts expose cast value identities across use sites | The lower-MIR artifact now has explicit coverage that cast pointer values keep the stable `value_id=cast` identity across return checks, local initializers, assignments, call arguments, aggregate fields, and aggregate elements. | C consumes MIR no-overflow facts for nested unchecked operands | C lowering now materializes nested `unchecked.add` / `unchecked.sub` / `unchecked.mul` operands inside an enclosing MIR-proven no-overflow expression instead of sending them through the generic builtin-call path. | C/LLVM call-produced pointer-member aggregate copies lower recursively | Aggregate member value loads/stores reached through call-produced pointer bases now have explicit C and LLVM evidence. `external_outer().inner` and nested `external_nested_outer().middle.inner` reconstruct loads from race-tolerant scalar leaves and split stores into race-tolerant scalar leaf stores, proving the pointer-member aggregate path is not limited to named pointer parameters. | `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `call_pointer_member_aggregate_load` / `call_pointer_member_aggregate_store` / `call_nested_pointer_member_aggregate_load` / `call_nested_pointer_member_aggregate_store` in `lower-c pointer member aggregate value copies lower field-wise race-tolerantly`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` matching call-produced cases in `LLVM pointer-member aggregate value copies lower recursively`; focused C/LLVM pointer-member aggregate tests; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM slice scalar index access lowers race-tolerantly | Scalar and pointer-shaped element loads/stores through slice indexing now use unordered atomic LLVM access because the slice may refer to shared storage. Direct fixed local array indexing remains plain; aggregate slice elements remain a separate recursive whole-element access class. This is a bounded slice-index scalar access slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `scalarIndexUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `emitIndexLoad`, and `emitIndexAssignment`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM slice scalar index access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "slice scalar index"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM pointer-to-array scalar index access lowers race-tolerantly | Scalar and pointer-shaped element loads/stores through `pa.*[i]` now use unordered atomic LLVM access unless the pointer-to-array has a live `local_storage` proof. This preserves plain loads for local fixed-array aliases while covering ambiguous pointer-backed array storage. Aggregate whole elements remain a separate recursive access class. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `scalarIndexUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `pointerExprHasProvenLocalStorage`, `emitIndexLoad`, and `emitIndexAssignment`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM pointer-to-array scalar index access lowers race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "pointer-to-array scalar index"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM aggregate whole-element index access lowers recursively | Aggregate whole-element loads/stores through ambiguous slice storage and unproven pointer-to-array storage now reuse the recursive aggregate race-tolerant lowering path, reconstructing loaded elements from unordered atomic leaf loads and splitting stores into unordered atomic leaf stores. Proven-local pointer-to-array aggregate element loads and stores remain plain, and unsupported union-like leaves still fail closed through the shared helper. This is a bounded indexed aggregate whole-element slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `aggregateIndexUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `emitIndexLoad`, `emitIndexAssignment`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefLoad`, and `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefStore`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM aggregate whole-element index access lowers recursively` including `local_pointer_array_cell_load` / `local_pointer_array_cell_store`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "aggregate whole-element"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM indexed aggregate scalar fields lower race-tolerantly | Scalar fields reached through ambiguous indexed aggregate storage, such as `cells[i].value` and `pa.*[i].value`, now use unordered atomic LLVM access. Fixed local array aggregate field indexing remains plain. This is a bounded indexed aggregate-field scalar slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `scalarIndexedMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `indexedMemberRoot`, `emitMemberLoad`, and `emitMemberAssignment`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM indexed aggregate scalar fields lower race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "indexed aggregate scalar"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM nested indexed aggregate scalar member chains lower race-tolerantly | Nested scalar member chains rooted in ambiguous indexed aggregate storage, such as `cells[i].inner.value` and `pa.*[i].inner.value`, now have explicit regression coverage through the recursive indexed-member root detector. Fixed local array nested member loads remain plain. This is a bounded nested indexed-member scalar slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `scalarIndexedMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering` and `indexedMemberRoot`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM nested indexed aggregate scalar member chains lower race-tolerantly`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "nested indexed aggregate scalar"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively | Aggregate field value copies rooted in ambiguous indexed aggregate storage, such as `cells[i].inner` and `pa.*[i].inner`, now reuse the recursive aggregate race-tolerant lowering path. Loads reconstruct the aggregate from unordered atomic leaf loads, stores split the incoming aggregate into unordered atomic leaf stores, and fixed local array aggregate field loads remain plain. This is a bounded indexed aggregate-field value-copy slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `aggregateIndexedMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `indexedMemberRoot`, aggregate branches in `emitMemberLoad` / `emitMemberAssignment`, `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefLoad`, and `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefStore`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "indexed aggregate field value"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM nested indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively | Nested aggregate field value-copy chains rooted in ambiguous indexed aggregate storage, such as `cells[i].inner.leaf` and `pa.*[i].inner.leaf`, are covered by the same indexed-member root detection and recursive aggregate lowering path. Fixed local array nested aggregate field loads remain plain. This is a bounded nested indexed aggregate-field value-copy slice, not full closure of broader pointer-provenance race lowering. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `aggregateIndexedMemberBaseUsesRaceTolerantLowering`, `indexedMemberRoot`, and aggregate branches in `emitMemberLoad` / `emitMemberAssignment`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM nested indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "nested indexed aggregate field value"`; `git diff --check`. |
| LLVM local fixed-array indexed aggregate stores stay plain | Proven local fixed-array indexed aggregate stores now have explicit LLVM coverage alongside the race-tolerant ambiguous-indexed paths. Direct local `cells[i].value`, nested `cells[i].inner.value`, aggregate-field `cells[i].inner`, and nested aggregate-field `cells[i].inner.leaf` stores all lower with ordinary loads/stores and no atomics, proving the indexed-member race path does not over-apply to local stack arrays. | `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `local_array_member_store` / `local_array_nested_store` / `local_array_inner_store` / `local_array_leaf_store`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM indexed aggregate scalar fields lower race-tolerantly"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM nested indexed aggregate scalar member chains lower race-tolerantly"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM nested indexed aggregate field value copies lower recursively"`; `git diff --check`. |
| Union-like aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed | C and LLVM now have explicit coverage proving unproven pointer loads/stores of overlay-union and tagged-union aggregate values reject during backend emission rather than falling through to plain whole-object copies. This documents the current policy for union-like aggregate structural classes: fail closed until a sound bytewise or active-field race-tolerant lowering exists. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `emitRaceTolerantAggregateLoadFromPtr` / `emitRaceTolerantAggregateStoreFromPtr`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefLoad` / `emitRaceTolerantAggregateDerefStore`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed` overlay and tagged-union cases; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed` overlay and tagged-union cases; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed"`; `git diff --check`. |
| Union-like aggregate value-copy diagnostics are explicit | The overlay/C-union/tagged-union aggregate-copy policy now has source-spanned backend diagnostics in addition to fail-closed emission errors. C and LLVM reporter-backed tests prove unsupported union-like aggregate pointer deref copies surface `E_BACKEND_UNSUPPORTED` at the source expression instead of only returning a raw backend error. This closes the union-like aggregate value-copy matrix row by accepting fail-closed lowering with explicit diagnostics and fixture inventory. | `src/lower_c_emitter.zig` `reportUnsupportedIfNone`; `src/lower_llvm.zig` `reportUnsupportedIfNone`; reporter-backed cases in `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `lower-c union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed`; reporter-backed cases in `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `LLVM union aggregate pointer deref value copies fail closed`; focused C/LLVM union aggregate pointer-deref tests; `git diff --check`. |

| Move checker branch joins preserve moved field places | Branch cleanup no longer drops moved field places such as `p.a` when the root `p` belongs to the outer state. A field moved out in one branch and left live in another now reaches the branch join and reports `E_MOVE_BRANCH_MISMATCH`, instead of merging as if only the root binding mattered. This is a bounded CFG/place slice, not the full checker rewrite. | `src/sema_move.zig` `finalizeBranchLocals`, `mergeMoveBranches`, typed `moveSubplaceRootInOuter`, and `MovePlace` state; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_branch_partial_field_move`; direct `mcc check tests/spec/move_place.mc`; `zig build test`. |

| Move checker loops preserve moved field places | Loop analysis now detects moved field-place state created by a `while` condition or loop body, such as `consume(p.a)`, and reports `E_MOVE_LOOP_RESOURCE` because the loop may run zero or multiple times. `while` condition and body forward transfer now use production CFG worklist blocks, with the existing loop-specific widening preserving the diagnostic and poison state. This is a bounded alias-reassignment slice, not full unknown pointer-pointee ownership modeling. | `src/sema_move.zig` assignment re-derive path using `callLaunderedMoveReferent`, `AliasReferent`, and typed `MovePlace` referents; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_reassigned_laundered_field_alias_after_move` / `reject_reassigned_laundered_array_element_alias_after_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker re-derives reassigned direct subplace aliases | Reassigning an existing pointer alias directly from `&pair.a` or `&arr[0]` now updates the alias referent and full-deref authority to the exact tracked subplace. Later reads after the subplace moves report `E_USE_AFTER_MOVE`, and moving through the reassigned alias consumes that field/element rather than losing the pointer-pointee relation or inheriting stale full-deref state from the old alias value. | `src/sema_move.zig` assignment re-derive path using `fullDerefMoveSubplace`, `AliasReferent`, `isDirectIdentAddressOf`, and `inheritedFullDerefAlias`; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `reject_reassigned_direct_field_alias_after_move` / `reject_reassigned_direct_array_element_alias_after_move` / `accept_reassigned_direct_field_alias_move_through` / `accept_reassigned_direct_array_element_alias_move_through`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker preserves copied full subplace aliases | Declaration-time copies of full pointer aliases to move subplaces now preserve both the exact referent and full-deref authority. Moving through `let q = p` where `p = &pair.a`, `p = &arr[0]`, or `p = &arr[i]` consumes the same field, concrete element, or wildcard element place instead of degrading to an unknown pointer read. The old formatted-subplace classifier has since been removed; current preservation flows through typed alias referents and `MovePlace` state. | `src/sema_move.zig` declaration alias copy path with `inheritedFullDerefAlias`, `AliasReferent`, and typed `MovePlace` referents; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_move_field_through_copied_full_alias` / `accept_move_array_element_through_copied_full_alias` / `accept_move_dynamic_array_element_through_copied_full_alias` / `reject_field_after_copied_full_alias_move` / `reject_array_element_after_copied_full_alias_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |
| Move checker tracks aliases assigned into uninitialized pointer storage | Assigning a move-subplace borrow into previously uninitialized pointer storage, such as `var pa: *Res = uninit; pa = &pair.a`, now creates the same precise alias slot as declaration-time and reassignment aliases. Direct field and constant-index element aliases, pointer-returning-call laundered field aliases, and dynamic multi-element array aliases are covered: moving through the pointer consumes the exact or wildcard subplace, and later pointer reads after that subplace moves report stale-alias `E_USE_AFTER_MOVE`. | `src/sema_move.zig` identifier assignment alias re-derive path creating a slot for untracked pointer targets; `tests/spec/move_place.mc` `accept_assigned_uninit_pointer_field_alias_move_through` / `reject_assigned_uninit_pointer_field_alias_after_move` / `accept_assigned_uninit_pointer_array_element_alias_move_through` / `reject_assigned_uninit_pointer_array_element_alias_after_move` / `accept_assigned_uninit_laundered_pointer_field_alias_before_move` / `reject_assigned_uninit_laundered_pointer_field_alias_after_move` / `accept_assigned_uninit_pointer_dynamic_array_element_alias_move_through` / `reject_assigned_uninit_pointer_dynamic_array_element_alias_after_move`; `zig test src/spec_tests.zig`; `zig test src/sema_tests.zig`; `git diff --check`. |

| Move checker tracks deferred borrow liveness | Deferred expressions that borrow move roots or subplaces now reserve that borrow separately from deferred consuming cleanup. | LLVM fixed pointer-array element updates consume MIR facts before fallback | Fixed local pointer-array element initializers and constant-index assignments now consult MIR pointer-provenance facts inside the shared element-cache helper before using backend-local AST inference. | C aggregate struct-literal pointer fields treat pointer containers as MIR-owned | C aggregate struct-literal pointer-field and pointer-array element helpers now use the shared direct pointer-container predicate, matching LLVM's typed-MIR ownership rule for pointer-local copies, raw-many zero-offset values, fixed-array element reads, and aggregate pointer reads. | C aggregate struct-literal reassignment local pointer-copy fields require MIR field facts | C now has scalar pointer-field parity with the existing pointer-array reassignment evidence. | Typed semantic facts cover nested same-struct aggregate copy pointer fields | Direct same-struct aggregate copy propagation now has explicit nested-field and nested pointer-array element evidence. MIR copies live `field_path` rows such as `inner.ptr` and `inner.ptrs[0]` from `outer` to `copied_outer`; C and LLVM consume those copied nested field facts for direct scalar derefs, while deleting the copied nested field or pointer-array element fact falls back to race-tolerant lowering without preserving a backend-only proof. | `src/mir_tests.zig` `from_copied_nested_field` / `from_copied_nested_field_element`; `src/lower_c_tests.zig` `c_nested_aggregate_field_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `c_nested_aggregate_array_element_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `copied` `inner.ptr` / `inner.ptrs` fact fixtures; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `nested_aggregate_field_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` / `nested_aggregate_array_element_copy_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `copied` `inner.ptr` / `inner.ptrs` fact fixtures; `zig test src/mir_tests.zig --test-filter "MIR records typed pointer provenance facts for direct globals and pointer arrays"`; `zig test src/lower_c_tests.zig --test-filter "lower-c aggregate pointer reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-field reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-array element reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`. |

| Lower-MIR artifact exposes nested aggregate copy field-path rows | The `lower-mir` dump now has explicit regression coverage for nested scalar `field_path` rows copied through same-struct aggregate initializer and assignment copies, not only the corresponding pointer-array element rows. | LLVM aggregate struct-literal pointer-copy fields require MIR field facts | LLVM no longer recreates local/global aggregate field provenance from backend-local pointer-copy inference when a direct struct-literal field value is already a MIR-owned pointer container expression but the matching `PointerProvenanceFact.field_path` row is missing. Direct pointer-copy, raw-many zero, noalias/direct address, pointer-array element, and aggregate pointer-field literal values now fail closed to unknown for direct aggregate field caches unless MIR supplies the field fact; the new local pointer-copy negative test proves a missing local `holder.ptr` fact falls back to unordered atomic lowering instead of preserving a backend-only local proof. | `src/lower_llvm.zig` `updateAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromStructLiteral`, `updateAggregateArrayPointerElementProvenanceFromLiteral`, `updateAggregatePointerFieldProvenanceFromAssignment`, and `directMirPointerContainerValueExpr`; `src/lower_llvm_tests.zig` `aggregate_field_local_pointer_copy_literal_direct_deref_requires_mir_field_fact` and missing `holder.ptr` fact fixture; `zig test src/lower_llvm_tests.zig --test-filter "LLVM aggregate pointer-field reads without MIR destination fact lower conservatively"`; `git diff --check`. |

| Move checker preserves symbolic bitwise-zero index identity | Identity-preserving bitwise expressions with zero now keep the same symbolic dynamic array place instead of falling back to an unknown dynamic/wildcard place. `i | 0`, `0 | i`, `i ^ 0`, and `0 ^ i` can move, reinitialize, and read the same dynamic move-resource element through the existing place model.
